# <a name="release-notes-for-office-insiders"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-103">Office 预览体验成员发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-103">Release Notes for Office Insiders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-104">本文包含 Windows 桌面版的 Word、Excel、PowerPoint、Outlook、Access 和 Project 的预览体验计划内部版本的发行说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-104">This article contains release notes for Insider builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, and Project for Windows desktop.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-105">每周，我们都会提供精彩集锦，其中包含我们希望你了解的有趣新功能、重要修补程序和所有重要问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-105">Every week, we'll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-106">注意，我们通常会在一段时间内向预览体验成员推出功能（有时甚至包括修补程序）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-106">Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Insiders over a period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-107">这可以让我们确保将功能向更多的受众发布之前，所用功能均可正常使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-107">This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-108">因此，如果你没有看到下面所述的功能，请不要担心，你最终会获取这些功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-108">So, if you don't see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span></span>  

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-109">发行说明每周发布一次，可能是多个版本的编译。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-109">Release notes are posted weekly and may be a compilation of multiple builds.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-110">发行说明发布日期可能与实际内部版本发布日期不一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-110">The release notes publication date may not match the actual build release date.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-111">Office 365 专业增强版现有安装的 Microsoft Teams - 从6月底开始, 将在更新这些安装的 Office 365 专业增强版 (和 Office 365 Business) 现有安装中包含 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-111">Microsoft Teams on existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus - Beginning in late June, Microsoft Teams will be included in existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus (and Office 365 Business) upon updates of these installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-112">将添加 Teams 的日期取决于所使用的更新频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-112">The date when Teams will be added depends on which update channel you're using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-113">有关详细信息, 请参阅[使用 Office 365 专业增强版部署 Microsoft Teams](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployoffice/teams-install)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-113">Please refer to [Deploy Microsoft Teams with Office 365 ProPlus](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployoffice/teams-install) for additional information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-117">*版本 2004（生成号 12718.20010）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-117">*Version 2004 (Build 12718.20010)*</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-119">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-119">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-120">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-120">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-121">**新增了用于在撰写邮件时禁用 @提及建议的选项：** 你是否觉得 @提及选取器更令人生厌，而不是更有用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-121">**New option to disable @ mention suggestions when composing mail:** Do you find the @ mention picker more annoying than useful?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-122">现在，可以根据需要禁用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-122">Now you can turn it off if you prefer.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-125">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-125">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-126">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-126">Outlook</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-127">修复了以下问题：附件工具中缺少“保存到云”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-127">Addresses an issue that caused the "Save to Cloud" button to be missing from Attachment Tools.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-128">修复了以下问题：如果用户对要回复的邮件没有所有者权限，在检查器窗口中回复受数字权限管理的邮件时，用户无法添加签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-128">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to add a signature when replying to a digitally rights managed message from an inspector window when the user does not have Owner permission on the message being replied to.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-129">修复了以下问题：用户无法将其他附件从 Web 位置添加到先前创建的会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-129">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to add additional attachments from a web location to a previously created meeting.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-130">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-130">PowerPoint</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-131">此更改修复了以下错误：无法保存包含表情符号的 PowerPoint 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-131">This change fixes an error that could cause PowerPoint files containing emojis to fail when saving.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-132">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-132">Project</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-133">修复了以下问题：在执行“CustomFieldValueListGetItem”时，如果自定义字段的查阅表格不存在，则会创建空的查阅表格，即使不应该创建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-133">Fixed an issue where if 'CustomFieldValueListGetItem' is executed and a lookup table for the custom field doesn't exist, an empty lookup table is created even though it should not be.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-134">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-134">Word</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-135">此更改修复了以下问题：在“视图”菜单中选择多个页面时，批注窗格可能会显示为空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-135">This change fixes an issue with multiple pages selected from the View menu, where the comments pane could be displayed as blank.</span></span>

## <a name="version-2004-march-20"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-137">版本 2004：3 月 20 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-137">Version 2004: March 20</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-138">*版本 2004（生成号 12711.20000）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-138">*Version 2004 (Build 12711.20000)*</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-140">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-140">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-141">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-141">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-142">**日历旧貌换新颜：** 去年，我们推出了全新的邮件体验；而今年，轮到日历改头换面了！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-142">**Calendar visual refresh:** Last year, we brought you a refreshed mail experience, and, this year, it is the calendar's turn to get a facelift!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-143">尽管这些更新是全新的，但却很熟悉。作为经验丰富的 Outlook 用户，你可以立即使用并提高工作效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-143">The updates are fresh but familiar so, as a seasoned Outlook user, you can jump in and be more productive right away.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-144">**帮助保护组中的数据：** 你在创建组时选择的敏感度标签应用于组电子邮件、文档和团队网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-144">**Help protect data in your group:** The Sensitivity label you choose when creating a group is applied to group email, documents, and team sites</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-145">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-145">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-146">**在幻灯片放映期间更新幻灯片：** 在演示期间更新其他作者更改的幻灯片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-146">**Update slides during slide show:** Update slides changed by other authors during your presentation.</span></span>

[//]: # (请勿移除功能详细信息内容结尾)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-149">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-149">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-150">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-150">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-151">此更改修复了以下问题：在处理包含格式不正确或无效协议信息的图片时出现延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-151">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-152">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-152">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-153">此更改修复了以下问题：在处理包含格式不正确或无效协议信息的图片时出现延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-153">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-154">此更改修复了以下问题：对电子邮件草稿的最新更改没有得到更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-154">This change fixes an issue where the latest changes to draft emails were not being updated.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-155">修复了以下问题：无法鼠标右键单击文件并使用“发送到”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-155">Fixed an issue where right-mouse clicking on a file and using 'Send to' would not work.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-156">修复了以下问题：如果用户有通讯簿的自定义搜索路径，Outlook 的名称解析范围会被限制为此自定义路径，而不包括全局地址列表 (GAL)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-156">Fixed an issue where if a user had a customized the search path for the Address book, Outlook's name resolution scope would be limited to the customized path rather than including the Global Address List (GAL).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-157">修复了以下问题：在一组返回的搜索结果中，按“类别”对结果排序时看不到“类别”颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-157">Fixed an issue where within a set of returned search results, sorting the results by Categories would not display the Category colors.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-158">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-158">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-159">修复了以下问题：当用户单击了“任务”功能区上“计划”分组中的“停用”按钮后，“ProjectBeforeTaskChange”Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件未触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-159">Fixed an issue where the 'ProjectBeforeTaskChange' Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event did not fire when a user clicked the "Inactivate" button found on the Tasks Ribbon within the Scheduling grouping.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-160">如果你在“窗体类型”视图中设置前置任务或后续任务详细信息，ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件并不总是能够捕获更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-160">If you set predecessor or successor details from within a Form type view, the ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event didn't always capture the changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-161">例如，如果你删除了依赖项，并单击了窗体上的“确定”，但此事件并未触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-161">For example, if you deleted a dependency and clicked OK on the form, the event did not fire.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-162">此行为已修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-162">This behavior has been fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-163">修复了以下问题：在你更改（如更改日期）后，“已完成工作量的实际成本(ACWP)”的最新值不会显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-163">Fixed an issue where the latest values for the Actual Cost of Work Performed (ACWP) would not be displayed after making a change, such as a date change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-164">修复了以下问题：使用“最近经常使用(MRU)”菜单打开项目时，打开的是带有读/写访问权限的项目文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-164">Fixed an issue where opening a project using the Most Recently Used (MRU) menu opened the project file with Read/Write access.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-165">此更改修复了以下问题：如果你创建的手动任务包含开始日期和时间（但没有持续时间），它会在时间线上显示不正确的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-165">This change fixes an issue where if you created a manual task with a start date and a time (but no duration), it would be displayed with an incorrect time on the timeline.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-166">修复了以下问题：使用回历打印时间线会导致在打印视图中跳过或重复某个月。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-166">Fixed an issue where printing a timeline using Hijri calendar would result in a month being skipped or duplicated in the print view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-167">此更改修复了以下问题：在工作组规划器中使用 GDI 对象时，可能会导致 GDI 对象的过度分配，并导致内存不足。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-167">This change addresses an issue where working in Team Planner with GDI objects, could result in the over allocation of GDI objects and create low memory conditions.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-168">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-168">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-169">修复了以下问题：评论发布功能已遭禁用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-169">Fixed an issue where the functionality to post comments was disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-170">此更改修复了以下问题：在处理包含格式不正确或无效协议信息的图片时出现延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-170">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-171">此更改修复了以下问题：帐户管理员不会分派消息，导致第三方应用程序挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-171">This change addresses an issue where the account manager would not dispatch messages resulting in a hang with third party applications.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-172">此更改修复了以下问题：目录会使用文档中没有的标题样式进行更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-172">This change fixes an issue where the Table of Contents would get updated with heading styles which were not present in the document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-173">修复了以下问题：当你通过邮件发送文档时，保存在 Word 文档中的数字签名会遭删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-173">Fixed an issue where digital signatures saved in Word documents would be removed when mailing the documents.</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT END)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-190">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-190">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-199">修复了禁用“可用时显示用户照片”选项时，搜索不显示有关用户的信息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-199">Fixed an issue where search shows no information about users when the option to "Show user photographs when available" is disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-207">修复了标记涉及公式的修订后可能导致保存文件失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-207">Fixed an issue where marking revisions involving equations could result in a failure when saving the file.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-464">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-464">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-465">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-465">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-466">**高级组电子邮件设置：** 此功能可帮助组用户自定义要在收件箱中接收/关注的电子邮件或事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-466">**Advanced group email settings:** This feature helps groups users to customize which emails or events to receive/follow in their inbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-467">**组命名策略：** 组命名策略使 IT 管理员能够标准化管理组织中由用户创建的组名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-467">**Groups Naming policy:** A group naming policy enables the IT admin to standardize and manage the names of groups created by users in the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-468">管理员可以要求在创建组时向名称添加特定前缀和后缀，并阻止使用指定的字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-468">The admin can require a specific prefix and suffix be added to the name for a group when it's created, and can block specific words from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-469">这有助于尽可能在组名中减少使用不适宜的字词，以及有助于IT部门在目录中管理组的显示方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-469">This helps minimize the use of inappropriate words in group names as well as IT manage the representation of groups in their directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-470">命名策略还可有助于组织根据部门部署团队网站，以进行分类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-470">Naming Policy also helps organizations that deploy team sites to categorize them based on department.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-471">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-471">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-472">**制表符窗格：** 现在，可以使用应用程序右侧的选项卡 UI 在多个窗格之间进行切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-472">**Tabbed Panes:** Now you can switch between multiple panes using a tab UI on the right hand side of the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-473">UI 将只在当打开2个以上的窗格时才会可见。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-473">The UI will only be visible when you have 2+ panes open.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-561">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-561">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-562">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-562">Excel</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-563">**将上下文和 SVG 对象一起显示！：** 现在，你可以在 Office 中转换这些对象时保留地图、图表和其他 SVG 向量中的文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-563">**Bring the context along with your SVG objects!:** Now you can retain the text in maps, chart and other SVG vectors when converting these objects in Office.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-564">**选择 Surface 触控笔时查看触控笔选项：** 首次在 Word、Excel 或 PowerPoint 中选取 Surface 触控笔时，将激活“绘图”选项卡，以轻松选择笔颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-564">**See Your Pen Options When You Pick Up Your Surface Pen:** When you first pick up your Surface Pen in Word, Excel, or PowerPoint, the Draw tab will be activated to make selecting your pen colors easy.</span></span>

## <a name="june-21-2019"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1106">2019 年 6 月 21 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1106">June 21, 2019</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1107">版本 1907（生成号 11815.20002）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1107">Version 1907 (build 11815.20002)</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1108">新变化：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1108">What's New:</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1109">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1109">Outlook</span></span>

#### <a name="dark-mode-for-black-theme-in-outlook-desktop"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1110">Outlook Desktop 中黑色主题的深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1110">Dark Mode for Black Theme in Outlook Desktop</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1111">在深色模式下，使用黑色主题的用户现在还可以在阅读电子邮件时看到有深色背景的阅读窗格，并在撰写电子邮件时看到有深色背景的撰写窗格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1111">With dark mode, users in black theme will now also see the reading pane with a dark background when reading emails, and the compose experience with a dark background when writing emails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1112">阅读窗格和功能区上有“太阳/月亮”切换，以防用户想要改用浅色背景来预览邮件外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1112">There is a sun/moon toggle on the reading pane and in the ribbon in case users want to preview what the message looks like with a light background instead.</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1113">开始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1113">Getting Started:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1114">黑色主题和深色模式默认处于启用状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1114">Turn on black theme and dark mode will be on by default.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1115">用户可以使用阅读窗格和功能区上的“月亮/太阳”切换，在浅色模式下预览邮件外观</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1115">Use the moon/sun toggle (in the reading pane and in the ribbon) to preview what the message looks like for users not in dark mode</span></span>

#### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1116">可尝试的方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1116">Scenarios to Try</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1117">在深色模式下阅读电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1117">Read emails in dark mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1118">如果你无法阅读某些内容，请使用“阅读窗格”中的太阳切换按钮切换为浅色背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1118">If you are unable to read something, use the sun toggle in the Reading Pane to switch to a light background.</span></span> 
2. <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1119">在深色模式下撰写电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1119">Compose emails in dark mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1120">使用功能区中的太阳切换按钮，在浅色背景下预览邮件的显示效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1120">Preview what your message will look like with a light background by using the sun toggle in the ribbon.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1121">如果遇到任何无法正常呈现的电子邮件，请将它们作为附件发送到 OutlookDarkModeFail@service.microsoft.com</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1121">If you encounter any emails that don't render properly, please send them (as an attachment) to OutlookDarkModeFail@service.microsoft.com</span></span>

#### <a name="get-location-suggestions"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1122">获取位置建议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1122">Get location suggestions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1123">开始键入内容，Outlook 将会搜索匹配的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1123">Start typing and Outlook will look for matching locations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1124">这适用于在创建约会和会议时看到的“位置”字段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1124">This applies to the Location field when creating Appointments and Meetings.</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1125">开始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1125">Getting Started:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1126">在 Outlook 的 O365 或 Outlook.com 日历上创建约会或会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1126">Create an Appointment or Meeting on an O365 or Outlook.com calendar in Outlook.</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1127">单击“位置”字段，并开始键入内容…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1127">Click into the Location field and start typing…</span></span>

#### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1128">可尝试的方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1128">Scenarios to Try</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1129">向会议添加会议室时，单击“位置”字段，而不是使用“会议室查找器”加载项或通讯录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1129">When adding a conference room to a meeting, click into Location field, rather than using Room Finder add-in or Address Book.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1130">对于在有公共位置的实体场所（比如餐馆、咖啡店或甚至是牙医诊所）进行的约会，试着用新的选取器来查找确切位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1130">For appointments at a physical place with a public location - like a restaurant, coffee shop, or even your dentist's office - try finding the exact location using the new picker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1131">这样一来，就可以在要离开时收到 Outlook Mobile 通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1131">This way, you'll be able to get notified on Outlook Mobile when it's time to leave.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1198">新增功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1198">What's New:</span></span>

#### <a name="dialog-for-contacting-support-now-is-dockable-and-appears-on-the-right"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1200">用于联系支持人员的对话框现可停靠且显示在右侧</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1200">Dialog for Contacting Support now is dockable and appears on the right</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1201">用于联系支持人员的对话框现将显示在右侧窗格且作为停靠的窗口启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1201">The dialog used for Contacting support will now appear in a pane on the right and will start off as a docked window.</span></span>

#### <a name="ink-in-your-email"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1202">电子邮件中的墨迹功能！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1202">Ink in Your Email!</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1204">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1204">Word</span></span>

#### <a name="open-document-links-in-word"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1205">在 Word 中打开文档链接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1205">Open document links in Word</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1206">单击 Office 中的文档链接时，可更新要在 Word 应用中的默认打开的首选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1206">When you click a document link in Office, you can update your preference to open in the Word app by default.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1207">要更新首选项，请转到“文件”->“选项”->“高级”->“链接处理”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1207">To update your preference go to File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1208">了解详细信息：https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1208">Learn more: https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span></span>

##### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1209">开始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1209">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1210">功能默认关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1210">Feature will default to off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1211">用户可通过“选项”->“高级”->“链接处理”设置将其启用，也可在 Win32 WXP 应用引导其使用“选择加入”体验时选择加入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1211">Users can either turn it on via Options->Advanced->Link Handling setting, or they can opt-in when Win32 WXP apps take them through an opt-in experience.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1212">当用户通过 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 单击 OneDrive/OneDrive for Business/SharePoint 上存储的 Word/PowerPoint/Excel 文件的链接时，这些链接将在相应的 Office 应用程序中打开，而不是默认在浏览器中打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1212">When users click on links to Word/PowerPoint/Excel files stored on OneDrive/OneDrive for Business/SharePoint from Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel, these links will open in the appropriate Office application instead of the browser by default.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1213">要更改此默认设置，用户可在 Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中更新以下设置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1213">To change this default, users can update the following setting in Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1214">“文件”->“选项”->“高级”->“链接处理”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1214">File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1215">此设置跨 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 共享，且可在上述任一应用中进行设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1215">This setting is shared across Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel and can be set in any of these apps.</span></span>

##### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1216">可尝试的方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1216">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1217">要触发“选择加入”体验 - 请通过 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 打开 OneDrive/SharePoint 中存储的 Word 文档的链接（通过 Office Online 在客户端中单击“打开”），在 30 天的时间段内执行此操作两次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1217">To trigger the opt-in experience - Open a link tot a Word document stored in OneDrive/SharePoint from Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel - click on Open in Client from Office Online - do this twice in a 30 day window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1218">选择加入后，链接将在 Win32 应用中默认启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1218">After you opt-in, links will launch in the Win32 apps by default.</span></span>

### <a name="morph-transition-enhancements---morph-by-name"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1671">平滑切换增强功能 - 按名称平滑</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1671">Morph Transition Enhancements - Morph by Name</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1672">选择需要平滑的形状</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1672">Specify the shapes you want to morph</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1673">入门：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1673">Getting Started:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1674">若要使“平滑”将两个对象视为同一对象，用户可以使用“选择窗格”来重命名形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1674">To get Morph to treat two objects as the same object, the user can rename the shapes using the Selection Pane.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1675">该名称必须以“!!”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1675">The name must be prefaced with "!!"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1676">（两个感叹号）开头，以便“平滑”使用它来覆盖默认匹配行为，例如“!!Name”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1676">(two exclamation points) for Morph to use it to override our default matching behavior, e.g. "!!Name"</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1677">用户可以使用任何不是以“!!”开头的名称来重命名形状，</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1677">Users can continue to rename shapes with any name that doesn't start with "!!"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1678">不必担心这会改变 Morph 的工作方式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1678">without worrying that it will change the way Morph works</span></span>

#### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="9a79b-1679">可尝试的方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a79b-1679">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>
